Uniply Industries Limited    UNIPLY : Updates UNIPLY : Uniply Industries Limited has informed the Exchange regarding 'Non-submission of Annual Reports for the year ended March 2020.'.

Dear Madam / Sir,

We regret to inform you that the submission of annual reports and conducting annual general meeting of the Company for the year ended March 2020 is getting delayed. As informed from time to time this delay is on account of continuous health issue of our sole executive Director Mr. Keshav Narayan Kantamnei and due to the enormous scale of the problem Company is facing on account of ongoing Covid Pandemic.

However, we wish to inform you that the Board has taken all necessary steps to conduct audit of accounts and annual general meeting. We will be able to submit the annual report by 1st week of January 2021 and AGM by end of January, 2021.

We further inform you that we will also seek the permission of ROC, Chennai, Tamilnadu for extension of date of AGM.

In view of the above we request you to kindly condone the delay in submission of annual report and allow us to conduct the AGM by January 2021.

We regret for the inconvenience.
